<Review>I have been shopping at their Dublin store since they opened a couple years ago. This one is less than a year old. Carry the same stuff, different store layout. The staff is not as friendly, more low key.

If you never been to a Sprouts, you must. It's like if Whole Foods and Trader Joes had a love child, this is what it would look like. Like a Whole Foods, but at Trader Joes prices. Extensive bulk food selection (roasted salted okra, coconut flour, macadamia nuts, all kinds of candy, including sugar free).

I love their fresh fruits and vegetables selection (organic and conventionally grown) and fresh meat counter. Not as extensive as Lunardi's, but I do buy my fresh turkey every year for Thanksgiving at Sprouts. Large house made chicken and pork sausage selection. You can request any sausage to be made bulk.

7/15/17 Update: Very impressed! To encourage kids to eat fresh fruit and a lifetime of eating healthy, Sprouts is now offering at kids height-self-serve free fresh fruit in the produce area. NIce!<//Review><Time>1500142053002<//Time>< user_name>

< Text>
Great food.  Great Sandwiches from the Deli.  The absolute worst business I have ever dealt with when it comes to answering and helping customers on the phone.  If you call this store to order a sandwich from the Deli, you most likely will sit on the phone for 15+ minutes if you have the patience to wait.  Just out of curiosity, while working at my desk, I tried to do an endurance test to see how long I could hold out and I have been on hold on the phone with this store for over 40 minutes.  I'm not sure if their phones have an audible ring.

*EDIT 8/29/19* Just an update after multiple years for comparison and to see if there has been any improvement to this area of criticism.

Still atrocious.   Its clear that there are members of the staff that have no interest in customer service.   An attempt to speak to someone on the phone in the deli was made 5 times.
First attempt:  Clerk answered the phone and happily transferred me to the deli.   The Deli then picked up the line and immediately hung up.
Second attempt: Line rings, is answered and then is hung up.
Third attempt: Clerk answered the phone, apologized that I was hung up on (when mentioned *not aggressively, just matter of fact) requested I stay on the line and he'd have someone get right with me.   The Deli picked up the line a short while later, and then immediately hung up.
Fourth attempt: Line rings, is answered and then is hung up.
Fifth attempt: Line rings, is answered and then is hung up.

I would also like to note that each time the line was picked up and hung up, it wasn't immediate.  It was clearly manual as I could hear background noises of the store before the end 'click'.

This is not a big deal because I can take my business elsewhere.  I like the sprouts chain, however, trying to deal with the San Ramon branch is the equivalent of inflicting pain on myself.

It should be noted that the service standards of this location have not improved any over 3-4 years and the staff (at least part of it) has absolutely no interest in putting any effort into what they were hired for.< /Text>

<Review>This place is similar in concept to a Panda Express - pick any 2/3 protein items, add starch, etc - but, the food is anything but. I got a small bowl with spicy tuna and salmon and a bunch of veggies (you can get as many as you want) with brown rice. The rice was a bit dry (as brown rice is often wont to be), but otherwise the mix was excellent. The person preparing my meal suggested keeping the spicy tuna separate from the salmon (normally they mix everything together by hand). I am not sure that made much of a difference since I was eating all of them together.
Overall, a good experience and I am certainly inclined to go back again.< /Review>< time>

<user>116693977047817765625< /user>< name>
Marion Soriano<//name>

< text>
Food : Out of all the revolving sushi bars I have been to, this restaurant possibly could have the best quality fish. Their fish is very fresh if your order it through server or the  list paper they provide you to turn in. I have not seen too many places with Escolar, so it was fantastic to see that they had this sushi/sashimi. Also, keep your eye out for their  daily deals on their hand rolls; it's definitely a steal.

Service/Environment: Their service is pretty quick. Although, due to popularity, you should expect a wait during peak hours.

Price: Price is definitely great for their sushi/sashimi. But with their price definitely expect the presentation to be just average. They charge you depending on the plate the sushi/sashimi comes in, so just be aware how much you accumulate because it does add up quickly!

Overall: Kaisen Sushi Bar has got to be my favorite revolving sushi bar. It definitely is my go to for after work dinner. It is the kind of place where you feel comfortable eating by yourself or with a group. They have incredible fresh fish and huge variety of food for a very reasonable price. Just note that its not the cleanest sushi bar around, but it definitely is worth going to!<//text>

Thursday is the day to go to Kaisen!

Everyday they have a hand roll special for $2.25 and on Thursdays it‚Äôs soft shell crab which my husband is a big fan of.

<username>S W.< /username><time>1467127605725<//time><Rate>5<//Rate>< Text>
Kaisen is one of my favorite sushi places around Orange County. Sure there's fancier ones but when sushi is floating around my head around dinner time, Kaisen is where I'm headed.

It's great eating alone or for smaller parties (2-3) since the majority of seating is at the rotating sushi bar. There are tables that seat up to 4 comfortably but the wait for those are usually pretty long.

I highly recommend getting the Kaisen roll and salmon nigiri.</Text>

< review>
Absolutely incredible value. Everything is delicious and you get much higher quality than the prices would suggest. This is a revolving sushi bar so all items are made in the kitchen and rotate around on a conveyor belt for you to select at will, with an option to place special orders. Different plates are worth different prices -  there's a guide on the wall.  You get charged based on the colors of the inevitable plate tower you build as you eat. Keep your eye on the specials of the day and order a few from there.  The sea chicken is deceptively good for something so simple.<//review>

<Text>Kaisen is one of my favorite sushi bars in Santa Ana. The restaurant is little on the small side seating about 40 or 50 people but it's worth the wait. It's located right off Bristol and Sunflower in the Staples shopping center.

This is a rotating sushi bar with daily specials. My favorite time of the week to go is on Mondays. $1.75 for Tuna hand rolls! I have been here so many times, I know the specials for each day, kind of funny and sad. Kaisen also has everyday specials like the Salmon Skin hand roll and the Negitora roll. The best place to sit is either at booths or close to the sushi chefs because you will get you're food faster.

I have never had a problem with the food. At times, the sushi on rotating belt can look dehydrated but just order directly off the menu if you want it. The Kaisen roll is one of my favorites -- 5 piece with spicy tuna, shrimp and the rolls are huge.

Service also great. Waitresses are rotating around the restaurant, ensuring your water is full or if you need something off the menu. The prices are very affordable. Menu items range from .99 to $9 depending on what you order. Give it a go and enjoy some delicious affordable sushi!<//Text>< rating>
4<//rating>

I was very excited about this place because I had heard good things. But my experience here was not great. The food itself is pretty good quality. The first round of food got to us within ten minutes. The second order never got to us even after talking to the waitress. We forgot to put our table number on our order form but immediately notified the waitress and she said she would take a look in the kitchen to see if they have it and that she would correct the problem but never returned or notified us that the issue had been resolved. My boyfriend and I sat there for twenty minutes waiting to hear something from the waitress or at least for our food to come out on the revolving bar. But nothing. The waitresses aren't attentive at all and will only come up to you if you call them over. After asking another waitress about our food she went to check the kitchen and claimed there was no order back there. We asked for the check instead. When we got the check, we were charged for a pricier item that we didn't order but paid for it because we didn't want anymore problems. During the entire meal, the only grab items that were on the conveyor belt were salmon sushi, seaweed salad, and edamame. Although we don't think they were deserving a tip, we still left one. Overall, I don't think I will return.</Text>
